Magic Origins RTPQ Kyoto
========================



 Posted in [ARCHIVES](/en/articles/archive)
 on July 10, 2015

By Wizards of the Coast










* [Pro Tour *Battle for Zendikar* Regional Pro Tour Qualifier Top 8 Decklists](http://magic.wizards.com/en/articles/organized-play/the-pro-tour-main-stage-2015-07-10)


Thanks to [Yellow Submarine](http://www.yellowsubmarine.co.jp/) for organizing this Regional Pro Tour Qualifier and submitting Top 8 decklists!
